The 6-foot-4, 225-pounder showed elusiveness and a big stiff-arm to get into the end zone. That was by far the biggest highlight Humphrey has made so far this summer -- and it enters him into the race for one of those final WR roster spots with fellow hopefuls like Emmanuel Butler, Simmie Cobbs Jr. and Cyril Grayson Jr., who started flashing early in training camp. Butler, who missed the past week with an unspecified injury after his early star turn, must be itching to get back on the field.</p></div><div class="now-feed_item-meta display-share" data-src="http://www.espn.com/espn/now?nowId=21-41072727-4" data-original-src="http://www.espn.com/espn/now?nowId=21-41072727-4">
